# Semantic Query Deep Dive

  <TraceChatBubble

<div className="ce-semantic-deepdive-chip-row">
  <span className="ce-semantic-chip">Text -> Intent -> SQL</span>
  <span className="ce-semantic-chip">Java + LLM + DB</span>
  <span className="ce-semantic-chip">Read-only guardrails</span>
</div>

:::tip Deep-dive Mode
This page is intentionally long and practical. Read sections in order for best understanding.
:::

This document is a detailed technical deep dive of ConvEngine semantic query runtime, from user question to final answer.

Primary example used repeatedly:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
find all requests where notes text says cancelled due to duplicate
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


One-line architecture:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
User text -> CanonicalIntent -> Safe SQL -> Postgres execution -> Final answer
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


---

## 1. Mental model first (must lock this)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 1. Mental model first (must lock this)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "1. Mental model first (must lock this)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

If this one section is clear, everything else in this document becomes easy.

- The planner does orchestration.
- Agent-1 does meaning extraction.
- Agent-2 does SQL compilation under constraints.
- Postgres executes parameterized SQL.
- Response layer converts rows into answer text.

This is not naive text-to-SQL.

This is text-to-intent-to-SQL with guardrails.

### 1.1 What changed in refined semantic runtime

Old weak model (what usually fails):

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
Question -> one LLM call -> SQL -> execute
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Refined model (ConvEngine semantic flow):

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
Question
  -> planner tool chain
  -> db.semantic.interpret (CanonicalIntent)
  -> db.semantic.query (SQL + params + guardrails)
  -> postgres.query
  -> final answer
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 1.2 Why this split matters

- ambiguity is handled before SQL generation
- SQL generator receives stable structure
- mapping and validation can enforce allowed columns
- read-only guardrails protect database
- failure memory improves retries

---

## 2. End-to-end chain in plain English

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 2. End-to-end chain in plain English"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "2. End-to-end chain in plain English",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

1. user asks a business question
2. planner routes to semantic chain
3. Agent-1 interprets meaning and emits CanonicalIntent
4. Agent-2 compiles read-only SQL from CanonicalIntent
5. SQL is validated against mapping and policy
6. postgres executes with named parameters
7. rows are synthesized into final answer

You can think of this as:

- planner = traffic controller
- interpret = business meaning resolver
- query = constrained SQL compiler
- postgres = execution engine

---

## 3. Who owns what (Java vs LLM vs DB)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 3. Who owns what (Java vs LLM vs DB)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble

    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "3. Who owns what (Java vs LLM vs DB)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

### 3.1 Ownership matrix

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["Concern", "Primary owner", "Secondary constraint"]}
  rows={[
    ["Turn orchestration", "Java", "planner config tables"],
    ["Entity/queryClass/filter understanding", "LLM (Agent-1)", "semantic metadata tables"],
    ["SQL draft generation", "LLM (Agent-2)", "mapping + failure memory + guardrails"],
    ["Safety checks", "Java", "SQL guardrail config + mapping"],
    ["Data retrieval", "Postgres", "JDBC named params"],
    ["Final wording", "Java/LLM response layer", "rows returned"]
  ]}
/>


### 3.2 If output is wrong, who likely decided it?

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["Symptom", "Likely decision point"]}
  rows={[
    ["wrong entity", "Agent-1 interpretation"],
    ["wrong filter field", "Agent-1 interpretation or missing mapping"],
    ["wrong join", "Agent-2 SQL generation"],
    ["wrong column name", "Agent-2 SQL generation or stale mapping"],
    ["SQL blocked", "Java guardrail validation"],
    ["empty result for valid question", "business data mismatch or too strict filter"]
  ]}
/>

      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",

      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"

### 5.1 CanonicalIntent (core object)

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "entity": "DisconnectRequest",
  "queryClass": "LIST",
  "filters": [
    {
      "field": "notesText",
      "op": "CONTAINS",
      "value": "cancelled due to duplicate"
    }
  ],
  "sort": [
    { "field": "createdAt", "dir": "DESC" }
  ],
  "limit": 100
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 5.2 SemanticQueryResponse (shape idea)

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "compiledSql": {
    "sql": "SELECT ...",
    "params": {
      "notesText": "%cancelled due to duplicate%",
      "__limit": 100
    }
  },
  "guardrail": {
    "readOnly": true,
    "mappingValid": true
  },
  "meta": {
    "retryAttempt": 0,
    "needsClarification": false,
    "unsupported": false
  }
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>

## 6. Core semantic tables and exactly what they do

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 6. Core semantic tables and exactly what they do"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "6. Core semantic tables and exactly what they do",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

### 6.1 `ce_semantic_concept`

Purpose:

- allowed business entities
- anchors for interpretation

Sample rows:

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["concept_code", "description"]}
  rows={[
    ["DisconnectRequest", "Customer disconnect request"],
    ["DisconnectOrder", "Downstream disconnect order"],
    ["Account", "Account master"],
    ["SubAccount", "Sub account"],
    ["Connection", "Physical connection"],
    ["Billing", "Billing context"],
    ["Payment", "Payment context"],
    ["SupportTicket", "Support context"],
    ["Installation", "Install context"],
    ["ServicePlan", "Plan context"]
  ]}
/>


Contribution in example:

- helps Agent-1 choose `DisconnectRequest`

### 6.2 `ce_semantic_synonym`

Purpose:

- language normalization
- map user words to canonical terms

Sample rows:

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["synonym", "maps_to"]}
  rows={[
    ["requests", "DisconnectRequest"],
    ["disconnect request", "DisconnectRequest"],
    ["notes", "notesText"],
    ["comments", "notesText"],
    ["remarks", "notesText"],
    ["cancelled", "cancelled"],
    ["duplicate", "duplicate"],
    ["failed", "FAILURE_ANALYSIS"],
    ["today", "TODAY"],
    ["last day", "LAST_24_HOURS"]
  ]}
/>


Contribution in example:

- helps resolve `notes text` to semantic field `notesText`

### 6.3 `ce_semantic_query_class`

Purpose:

- query shape contract

Sample rows:

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["query_class", "description"]}
  rows={[
    ["LIST", "list results"],
    ["FAILURE_ANALYSIS", "failure analytics"],
    ["COUNT", "count"],
    ["TREND", "trend"],
    ["SUMMARY", "summary"],
    ["DETAIL", "detail"],
    ["JOIN_VIEW", "join-heavy lookup"],
    ["ALERT", "alert lookup"],
    ["STATUS", "status lookup"],
    ["RECENT", "recent lookup"]
  ]}
/>


Contribution in example:

- query class selected as `LIST`

### 6.4 `ce_semantic_mapping`

Purpose:

- semantic field to physical table.column
- join bridge through shared keys
- validation boundary for SQL

Sample rows:

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["entity", "field", "table", "column"]}
  rows={[
    ["DisconnectRequest", "requestId", "zp_disco_request", "zp_request_id"],
    ["DisconnectRequest", "status", "zp_disco_request", "status"],
    ["DisconnectRequest", "createdAt", "zp_disco_request", "created_ts"],
    ["DisconnectRequest", "subAccountId", "zp_disco_request", "sub_account_id"],
    ["DisconnectRequest", "city", "zp_disco_request", "city"],
    ["DisconnectTransData", "requestId", "zp_disco_trans_data", "zp_request_id"],
    ["DisconnectTransData", "notesText", "zp_disco_trans_data", "notes_text"],
    ["DisconnectTransData", "action", "zp_disco_trans_data", "action"],
    ["DisconnectOrder", "orderId", "zp_disconnect_order", "order_id"],
    ["Account", "accountId", "zp_account", "account_id"]
  ]}
/>


Contribution in example:

- reveals `notesText` lives in `zp_disco_trans_data.notes_text`
- reveals join key `zp_request_id`

### 6.5 `ce_semantic_query_failures`

Purpose:

- failure memory for retry loop

Sample rows:

<DbTable
  title="Reference table"
  columns={["reason", "bad_sql", "corrected_sql"]}
  rows={[
    ["wrong table for notes", "r.notes_text", "t.notes_text"],
    ["missing join", "FROM zp_disco_request only", "JOIN zp_disco_trans_data t"],
    ["wrong join key", "r.id=t.id", "r.zp_request_id=t.zp_request_id"],
    ["weak filter", "LIKE '%cancelled%'", "ILIKE '%cancelled due to duplicate%'"],
    ["case mismatch", "LIKE", "ILIKE"],
    ["duplicate rows", "no DISTINCT", "SELECT DISTINCT"],
    ["missing limit", "no LIMIT", "LIMIT :__limit"],
    ["non read-only", "UPDATE/DELETE", "SELECT only"],
    ["invalid alias", "x.notes_text", "t.notes_text"],
    ["unmapped column", "notes", "notes_text"]
  ]}
/>


Contribution in example:

- nudges Agent-2 away from known SQL mistakes

## 7. One request, full trace, no ambiguity

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 7. One request, full trace, no ambiguity"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "7. One request, full trace, no ambiguity",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Question:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
find all requests where notes text says cancelled due to duplicate
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 7.1 Planner stage

What Java does:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
// planner picks tool chain
List<String> toolOrder = List.of(
  "db.semantic.interpret",
  "db.semantic.query",
  "postgres.query"
);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


What LLM does:

- not involved here

What DB does:

- planner config lookup (`ce_mcp_planner`, `ce_mcp_tool`)

### 7.2 Interpret stage

What Java does:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
List<SemanticConcept> concepts = semanticConceptRepository.findAllEnabled();
List<SemanticSynonym> synonyms = semanticSynonymRepository.findAllEnabled();
List<SemanticQueryClass> queryClasses = semanticQueryClassRepository.findAllEnabled();
List<SemanticMapping> mappings = semanticMappingRepository.findAllEnabled();

String systemPrompt = interpretPromptFactory.build(concepts, synonyms, queryClasses, mappings);
String userPrompt = "User question: " + question;
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


What LLM does:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
SemanticInterpretLlmOutput llmOut = llmClient.generateJsonStrict(
    systemPrompt,
    userPrompt,
    semanticInterpretOutputSchema
);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


What Java validates:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
CanonicalIntent intent = objectMapper.readValue(llmOut.json(), CanonicalIntent.class);
semanticConceptRepository.existsByConceptCode(intent.getEntity());
semanticQueryClassRepository.existsByQueryClass(intent.getQueryClass());
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Interpret output (typical):

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "entity": "DisconnectRequest",
  "queryClass": "LIST",
  "filters": [
    {
      "field": "notesText",
      "op": "CONTAINS",
      "value": "cancelled due to duplicate"
    }
  ],
  "limit": 100
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 7.3 Query stage

What Java does:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
List<SemanticMapping> sqlMappings = semanticMappingRepository.findAllEnabled();
List<SemanticQueryFailure> failures = semanticQueryFailureRepository.findRecent();
String sqlPrompt = semanticSqlPromptFactory.build(intent, sqlMappings, failures);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


What LLM does:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
SemanticSqlLlmOutput sqlOut = llmClient.generateJsonStrict(
    sqlPrompt,
    "Question: " + question,
    semanticSqlOutputSchema
);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


What Java validates:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
sqlGuardrail.assertReadOnly(sqlOut.getSql());
sqlValidator.validateAgainstMappings(sqlOut.getSql(), sqlMappings);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Candidate SQL:

<CodeBlockToggle title="SQL Example" language="sql" defaultOpen={true}>

```sql
SELECT DISTINCT
    r.zp_request_id,
    r.status,
    r.created_ts
FROM zp_disco_request r
JOIN zp_disco_trans_data t
  ON r.zp_request_id = t.zp_request_id
WHERE t.notes_text ILIKE :notesText
ORDER BY r.created_ts DESC
LIMIT :__limit;
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Params:

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "notesText": "%cancelled due to duplicate%",
  "__limit": 100
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 7.4 Execution stage

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
List<Map<String, Object>> rows = namedParameterJdbcTemplate.queryForList(
    sqlOut.getSql(),
    sqlOut.getParams()
);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 7.5 Final answer stage

- rows converted to natural language summary
- planner/response layer returns final output

---

## 8. Clarification path (when system should ask instead of guessing)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 8. Clarification path (when system should ask instead of guessing)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "8. Clarification path (when system should ask instead of guessing)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Ambiguous input example:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
show status for request 1001
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Ambiguity:

- request status?
- downstream order status?
- payment status?

Interpret result can be:

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "needsClarification": true,
  "clarificationQuestion": "Do you mean request status or downstream order status?",
  "ambiguities": ["requestStatus", "downstreamStatus"]
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Key rule:

- if clarification is required, pipeline should not proceed to SQL execution blindly

---

## 9. Unsupported path (safe refusal)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 9. Unsupported path (safe refusal)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "9. Unsupported path (safe refusal)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Example unsupported ask:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
delete all duplicate requests
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Desired behavior:

- semantic stage marks unsupported/write intent
- query stage refuses to compile executable write SQL

Expected meta shape:

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "unsupported": true,
  "unsupportedMessage": "Only read-only semantic queries are supported"
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


---

## 10. Guardrail path (read-only enforcement)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 10. Guardrail path (read-only enforcement)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "10. Guardrail path (read-only enforcement)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Blocked SQL patterns include:

- `INSERT`
- `UPDATE`
- `DELETE`
- `DROP`
- `TRUNCATE`
- `ALTER`
- `CREATE`
- multi-statement mutation attempts

Guardrail check pattern:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
sqlGuardrail.assertReadOnly(sql);
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


If blocked:

- write audit
- return safe error or unsupported state
- do not execute

---

## 11. Why the join appears in notes_text example

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 11. Why the join appears in notes_text example"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "11. Why the join appears in notes_text example",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Question says: notes text contains phrase.

Mapping says:

- base entity `DisconnectRequest` -> `zp_disco_request`
- field `notesText` -> `zp_disco_trans_data.notes_text`
- shared key `requestId` -> `zp_request_id`

Therefore SQL must include:

<CodeBlockToggle title="SQL Example" language="sql" defaultOpen={true}>

```sql
JOIN zp_disco_trans_data t
  ON r.zp_request_id = t.zp_request_id
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


Without this join, filter column is unresolved or wrong.

---

## 12. Why DISTINCT appears in many generated queries

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 12. Why DISTINCT appears in many generated queries"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "12. Why DISTINCT appears in many generated queries",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Failure memory may capture duplicate-row behavior when a request has multiple trans rows.

So generator learns:

- use `SELECT DISTINCT` where result cardinality can duplicate base entities

This is a quality and UX fix, not just syntax fix.

---

## 13. Method-level walk (simplified but practical)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 13. Method-level walk (simplified but practical)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "13. Method-level walk (simplified but practical)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

### 13.1 `DbSemanticInterpretToolHandler`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
public Object handle(Map<String, Object> args, EngineSession session) {
    SemanticInterpretRequest req = toInterpretRequest(args, session);
    return semanticInterpretService.interpret(req, session);
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 13.2 `SemanticInterpretService`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
public SemanticInterpretResponse interpret(SemanticInterpretRequest req, EngineSession session) {
    // 1) load semantic metadata
    // 2) build strict prompt
    // 3) call llm generateJsonStrict
    // 4) parse canonical intent
    // 5) validate against allowed metadata
    // 6) return meta + canonical intent
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 13.3 `DbSemanticQueryToolHandler`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
public Object handle(Map<String, Object> args, EngineSession session) {
    // canonicalIntent required in v2 flow
    SemanticQueryRequest req = toQueryRequest(args, session);
    return semanticLlmQueryService.query(req, session);
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


### 13.4 `SemanticLlmQueryService`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Java Example" language="java" defaultOpen={true}>

```java
public SemanticQueryResponseV2 query(SemanticQueryRequest req, EngineSession session) {
    // 1) load mappings + failure memory
    // 2) build SQL prompt
    // 3) call llm generateJsonStrict
    // 4) validate read-only + mapping compliance
    // 5) retry with failure context if needed
    // 6) return compiled sql + params
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>

## 14. SQL validation checklist (practical)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 14. SQL validation checklist (practical)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "14. SQL validation checklist (practical)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

Before execution, check all of these:

- SQL is read-only
- only allowed tables/columns appear
- selected columns map to known semantic fields
- join keys are valid
- params exist for placeholders
- limit exists and is bounded
- no unsafe function usage if policy blocks it

## 15. Debug cookbook (30-second diagnosis)

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 15. Debug cookbook (30-second diagnosis)"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "15. Debug cookbook (30-second diagnosis)",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

### 15.1 Wrong entity chosen

Check:

- concepts coverage
- synonym noise
- interpret prompt constraints
- clarification threshold too low/high

### 15.2 Wrong field chosen

Check:

- synonyms mapping quality
- field alias collisions
- mapping row correctness

### 15.3 Wrong join

Check:

- mapping keys for both entities
- relationship override/join hints
- failure memory not stale

### 15.4 SQL blocked unexpectedly

Check:

- guardrail pattern false positives
- generated SQL contains blocked token in comments/string

### 15.5 Empty results but query seems valid

Check:

- filter too strict
- value normalization mismatch
- date/timezone boundaries

---

  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "16. Operations notes for production",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

- keep semantic tables versioned and reviewed
- avoid ad-hoc mapping edits without tests
- monitor top failure reasons weekly
- backfill failure memory with corrected SQL examples
- maintain small high-signal synonyms, avoid noisy ones

## 17. Scholar-mode guided drills (appendix)

This appendix is intentionally long.

Each drill includes:

- question
- Java action
- LLM action
- DB action
- canonical intent shape
- SQL shape
- root-cause hints if output fails


### Drill 1

Question:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Question or Prompt" language="text" defaultOpen={true}>

```text
find all requests where notes text says cancelled due to duplicate
```

</CodeBlockToggle>

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="find all requests where notes text says cancelled due to duplicate"
    info={[
      "Drill input question",
      "Natural-language request",
      "Planner should route to semantic chain"
    ]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="ANALYZE"
    message="Running db.semantic.interpret -> db.semantic.query -> postgres.query for this drill."
    json={{
      mcp: {
        action: "CALL_TOOL",
        toolOrder: ["db.semantic.interpret", "db.semantic.query", "postgres.query"],
        semantic: { stage: "DRILL", mode: "read-only", pipeline: "text-to-intent-to-sql" }
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R)",
      "business tables (R)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Agent-1 resolves CanonicalIntent",
      "Agent-2 compiles SQL with mapping constraints",
      "Postgres executes named-parameter read-only SQL"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>


What Java does:

- loads semantic metadata and mappings
- builds strict prompt for interpret stage
- parses and validates CanonicalIntent
- builds strict prompt for query stage
- validates SQL with read-only + mapping checks
- executes parameterized SQL

What LLM does:

- Agent-1: chooses entity/query class/filter shape
- Agent-2: drafts SQL and params inside bounded context

What DB does:

- semantic tables provide constraints
- business tables provide final data rows

CanonicalIntent (expected shape):

<CodeBlockToggle title="JSON Example" language="json" defaultOpen={true}>

```json
{
  "entity": "DisconnectRequest",
  "queryClass": "LIST",
  "filters": [
    {
      "field": "notesText",
      "op": "CONTAINS",
      "value": "cancelled due to duplicate"
    }
  ],
  "limit": 100
}
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


SQL shape (expected):

<CodeBlockToggle title="SQL Example" language="sql" defaultOpen={true}>

```sql
SELECT ...
FROM zp_disco_trans_data t
WHERE t.notes_text = :p1
LIMIT :__limit;
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


If output is wrong, first checks:

1. Verify mapping row for `notesText` -> `zp_disco_trans_data.notes_text`
2. Verify query class constraints for `LIST`
3. Verify failure memory did not inject stale correction pattern
4. Verify guardrail did not strip/alter allowed SQL shape

```sql
FROM zp_disconnect_order t
WHERE t.order_id = :p1
LIMIT :__limit;
```

</CodeBlockToggle>


If output is wrong, first checks:

1. Verify mapping row for `orderId` -> `zp_disconnect_order.order_id`
2. Verify query class constraints for `DETAIL`
3. Verify failure memory did not inject stale correction pattern
4. Verify guardrail did not strip/alter allowed SQL shape

## 18. Final mental model to remember forever

<ChatContainer>
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="user"
    name="User"
    message="Explain: 18. Final mental model to remember forever"
    info={["Section walkthrough request"]}
  />
  <TraceChatBubble
    role="assistant"
    name="Semantic Agent"
    intent="SEMANTIC_QUERY"
    state="EXPLAIN"
    message="Section explanation with Java ownership, LLM boundaries, DB table usage, and trace expectations."
    json={{
      explain: {
        section: "18. Final mental model to remember forever",
        ownership: ["Java", "LLM", "DB"],
        guarantee: "read-only semantic runtime"
      }
    }}
    tables={[
      "ce_semantic_concept (R)",
      "ce_semantic_synonym (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_class (R)",
      "ce_semantic_mapping (R)",
      "ce_semantic_query_failures (R/W)"
    ]}
    info={[
      "Use this section to connect concept to runtime behavior",
      "Trace each decision point before debugging SQL",
      "Prefer clarification over guessing when ambiguity is high"
    ]}
  />
</ChatContainer>

- Java orchestrates.
- LLM interprets and drafts SQL.
- DB semantic tables constrain and validate.
- Postgres executes.
- Final answer is synthesized from rows.

If you keep this model, semantic runtime becomes predictable and debuggable.
